10:06 PM EDT</div></div><div class="article-body"><div class="teaser-content"><section><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">House investigators issued subpoenas Thursday to Energy Secretary Rick Perry and two associates of President Trumps personal lawyer Rudolph W. Giuliani, seeking key documents that have not been produced as part of the impeachment inquiry.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The subpoenas of the Giuliani associates, Lev Parnas and Igor Fruman, came after their arrests on campaign finance charges Wednesday night.</p></div></section></div><div class="remainder-content"><section><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump insisted that he did not know the two men, who are charged with scheming to funnel foreign money to U.S. politicians in a bid to affect U.S.-Ukraine relations. Both Parnas and Fruman have helped Giuliani investigate former vice president Joe Biden and his son, though the indictment does not mention Giuliani or suggest that he was part of the alleged crimes.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The developments played out as Trump prepared to head to Minneapolis for his first campaign rally since House Democrats launched the impeachment inquiry.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns dn db-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Meanwhile, Trumps woes continued to mount. According to people briefed on the matter, political appointees in the White House budget office intervened to freeze aid to Ukraine despite some career staffers raising concerns that the move was improper.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">And at least four national security officials were so alarmed by the Trump administrations attempts to pressure Ukraine that they raised concerns with a White House lawyer, people familiar with the matter said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"> Trumps Syria decision tests the bounds of Republican support as he <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trumps-syria-decision-tests-the-bounds-of-republican-support-as-he-demands-solidarity-on-impeachment/2019/10/09/b5f0c8b0-eaaa-11e9-85c0-85a098e47b37_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_10">demands solidarity on impeachment</a>.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_2"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"> Trumps <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trumps-broad-claims-of-executive-immunity-lead-to-criticism-he-is-acting-above-the-law/2019/10/09/b8811be8-eaaa-11e9-9c6d-436a0df4f31d_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_12">broad claims of executive immunity</a> lead to criticism he is acting above the law.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"> Whistleblowers lawyers say their client is <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/whistleblowers-lawyers-say-their-client-is-not-politically-motivated/2019/10/09/89baaba6-eade-11e9-9c6d-436a0df4f31d_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_13">not politically motivated</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/context/read-the-whistleblower-complaint-regarding-president-trump-s-communications-with-ukrainian-president-volodymyr-zelensky/4b9e0ca5-3824-467f-b1a3-77f2d4ee16aa/?tid=lk_inline_manual_14" title="www.washingtonpost.com">The whistleblower complaint </a>| <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/context/official-readout-president-trump-s-july-25-phone-call-with-ukraine-s-volodymyr-zelensky/4b228f51-17e7-45bc-b16c-3b2643f3fbe0/?tid=lk_inline_manual_14" title="www.washingtonpost.com">The rough transcript of Trumps call with Zelensky</a> |<a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/context/letter-from-white-house-counsel-pat-cipollone-to-house-leaders/0e1845e5-5c19-4e7a-ab4b-9d591a5fda7b/?tid=lk_inline_manual_14">The letter from White House counsel to House leaders</a></p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns dn db-ns relative" id="slug_inline_bb_2"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>9:00 p.m.: Trump takes aim at Biden, says Democrats impeachment effort will produce a backlash at the ballot box</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">At a raucous campaign rally  his first since Democrats began their impeachment inquiry  Trump predicted that his political opponents will pay a price at the ballot box, despite polls showing that a majority of the public supports impeaching him.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns db dn-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_3"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The Democrats brazen attempt to overthrow our government will produce a backlash at the ballot box, the likes of which they have never, ever seen before in the history of our country, Trump told the crowd in Minneapolis.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">A <a href="https://www.foxnews.com/politics/fox-news-poll-record-support-for-trump-impeachment">Fox News poll</a> released Thursday showed that 51 percent of voters want to see Trump impeached and removed from office. And despite Trumps claim of an attempt to overthrow our government, the impeachment process is established in the Constitution.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pad-top-md pad-bottom-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns dn db-ns relative" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_3"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump also launched a broadside against Biden and his son, Hunter.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Joe Biden was never considered smart, Trump said. I do not know what his business or legal activities in Ukraine have been.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>4:45 p.m.: Trump says he doesnt know Giuliani associates Parnas and Fruman</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">In an exchange with reporters outside the White House before departing for Minneapolis, Trump claimed he doesnt know Parnas and Fruman and dismissed a photo of himself together with the two men and Giuliani.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">I dont know those gentlemen, Trump said. Youd have to ask Rudy.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump also said he hopes Giuliani doesnt get indicted.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Asked whether he was serious when he <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-publicly-calls-on-china-to-investigate-bidens/2019/10/03/2ae94f6a-e5f2-11e9-b403-f738899982d2_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_131" title="www.washingtonpost.com">publicly asked China to investigate Biden last week</a>, Trump didnt answer directly  but his answer suggested that he did not make the comment in jest.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">China has to do whatever they want. If they want to look into something, they can look into it. If they dont ... they dont have to, Trump said, adding that it would be great either way.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">A number of prominent Republicans, including McCarthy, Sen. Marco Rubio (Fla.) and Rep. Jim Jordan (Ohio), have claimed that Trump was joking about the request to China.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>4 p.m.: House Democrats subpoena Energy Secretary Rick Perry</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Three House committees on Thursday subpoenaed Perry, giving him a deadline of Oct. 18 by which to produce key documents related to the impeachment inquiry.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The move by Intelligence Committee Chairman Adam B. Schiff (D-Calif.), Oversight and Reform Committee Chairman Elijah E. Cummings (D-Md.) and Foreign Affairs Committee Chairman Eliot L. Engel (D-N.Y.) comes just hours after the three chairmen issued subpoenas to Parnas and Fruman, the two Giuliani associates arrested Wednesday night.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">It also comes two days after the White House told Congress it would not cooperate with the inquiry.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Recently, public reports have raised questions about any role you may have played in conveying or reinforcing the Presidents stark message to the Ukrainian President, the lawmakers wrote <a href="https://oversight.house.gov/sites/democrats.oversight.house.gov/files/documents/2019-10-10.EEC%20Engel%20Schiff%20to%20Perry-DOE%20Joint%20Cover%20Letter%20re%20Subpoena.pdf" title="oversight.house.gov">in a letter to Perry</a>. These reports have also raised significant questions about your efforts to press Ukrainian officials to change the management structure at a Ukrainian state-owned energy company to benefit individuals involved with Rudy Giulianis push to get Ukrainian officials to interfere in our 2020 election.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">In a phone call with House Republicans last week, Trump emphasized that he had made a July 25 call with Ukrainian President Volodymyr Zelensky at the request of Perry. Trump said Perry urged him to contact Zelensky to discuss a liquefied natural gas project.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Energy Department spokeswoman Shaylyn Hynes said in an email last week that Perry absolutely supported and encouraged the President to speak to the new President of Ukraine to discuss matters related to their energy security and economic development.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>3:45 p.m.: Pompeo says Giuliani doesnt work for me</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Pompeo declined to say Thursday whether he thinks its inappropriate for Giuliani to have held meetings with Ukranian officials even though he is not on the State Department payroll.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">In an interview on Gray Televisions Full Court Press with Greta Van Susteren, Pompeo was asked whether Giuliani is an envoy, shadow secretary of state, or is he a personal lawyer in this Ukraine controversy. Pompeo first dodged the question.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">I run the State Department, he said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Pressed further, Pompeo declared that Giuliani doesnt work for me. Hes not on our payroll. Pompeo then told Van Susteren that she has the facts wrong on Giulianis actions, but he declined to go into the details here with you.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Its not uncommon for private citizens to help and inform U.S. government deliver its policy, Pompeo said. The ultimate responsibility falls to the United States government, for the secretary of state, to deliver on behalf of the outcomes President Trump has committed to the American people hed achieve.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>3:30 p.m.: Trump travels to liberal Minneapolis for his first rally since the impeachment probe began</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump is slated to travel to Minneapolis Thursday night to host a campaign rally and do what he often does when he feels threatened: seize on divisions in the country and try to split Americans into two distinct camps, those who are with him and those who are against him, with seemingly no middle ground allowed.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The event will allow him to fire up die-hard supporters at a time when polls suggest a majority of Americans are troubled by his conduct and favor the investigation.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">But unlike most of his rallies held in Republican strongholds, Trump selected a congressional district for Thursday nights event that he lost by 55 points in 2016  and one that is represented by Rep. Ilhan Omar (D-Minn.), the outspoken Somali American and Muslim lawmaker whom Trump has repeatedly attacked, sometimes using false information.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">It seems provocative. He wants to provoke a clash so he can arouse his cult to a civil war, said Polly Kellogg, 76, a retired social justice professor who plans to protest the rally. Hes looking for violent videos.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Read more <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-travels-to-liberal-minneapolis-for-his-first-rally-since-the-impeachment-probe-began/2019/10/10/85da135c-eac8-11e9-85c0-85a098e47b37_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_155" title="www.washingtonpost.com">here</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Jenna Johnson</i></p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>3:15 p.m.: Senate Democrats ask DOJ: Why didnt you investigate Trumps Ukraine call? </b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Democratic members of the Senate Judiciary Committee <a href="https://www.feinstein.senate.gov/public/_cache/files/2/3/2306e1d5-5d41-4083-9642-3150ddf32d88/5F6C5D7B433FA67A01A3CC1294CB1BCD.2019.10.10-benczkowski-letter.pdf" title="www.feinstein.senate.gov">sent a letter </a>to Assistant Attorney General Brian Benczkowski Thursday asking that he explain why the Justice Department decided not to investigate Trumps controversial call with the Ukrainian president.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">On its face, the White House memorandum of the July 25 call raises significant questions, including what was done following the call to follow through on the presidents requests, the senators wrote.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The Justice Department had instructed that the whistleblowers complaint not be given to Congress. After the White House released its transcript of the call, DOJ said it had determined it wasnt a campaign finance violation and said no further action was warranted.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Since this matter involves allegations about the Presidents conduct, and given this Presidents stated belief that he has the absolute right to do what I want to do with the Justice Department, it is important to ensure that the Department has acted in an objective, independent manner in declining even to investigate this matter, the Democrats wrote.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>2:30 p.m.: Sen. Gardner is latest GOP member who wont say if Trumps request to Ukrainian president was wrong</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Sen. Cory Gardner (R-Colo.) was asked repeatedly on Thursday to answer yes or no on the question of whether it was appropriate for Trump to ask a foreign leader to investigate a political rival.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Gardner refused to do so, blaming partisan politics for his unwillingness to answer, according to<a href="https://twitter.com/JoeStGeorge/status/1182355369001013248" title="twitter.com"> a video posted</a> by Joe St. George, the local Fox31 reporter who asked the questions.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Unfortunately what weve seen is a very political process takeover, Gardner said as he spoke with reporters in Colorado.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">When St. George tried to press him, Gardner said, I think Ive answered your question. But when he turned to the next reporter, she followed up: Is it yes or no?</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Gardner then a blamed the news media for focusing these questions on Colorado, Arizona, Maine and North Carolina (the four states where GOP incumbents are most vulnerable). It seems to be about politics and elections, Gardner said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">(As an aside, The Post is<a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/graphics/politics/trump-impeachment-gop-senators-reactions/?tid=lk_inline_manual_170" title="www.washingtonpost.com"> tracking all 53 GOP senators </a>on these questions.)</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">But the question is, is it appropriate? St. George tried again. Gardner dodged.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">St. George tried another way: Would you be okay with it if a Democrat asked a foreign government to investigate... No answer. Then he asked if itd be okay for the senator to ask a foreign government for help. No answer</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">By the end, St. George became exasperated.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">But youre not answering the question, we want to hear from you, youre a smart guy, you  know the debate, the reporter said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">This is about the politics of the moment, Gardner replied, still not answering the question.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>2:20 p.m.: GOP anger over Syria not translating to support for impeachment inquiry</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Rep. color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">While my votes will continue to support the presidents domestic policy agenda, because of this terrible foreign policy decision I asked that my name be Today, Minority Leader McCarthy and his campaign arm need to make a choice.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">This is a common tactic in congressional politics, where one side demands the other return money from donors who have conducted themselves in an illegal or unethical manner.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>1:15 p.m.: Trumps lawyer says president didnt know about allegations against Giulianis associates</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Jay Sekulow, a personal attorney for Trump, sought to distance his client from the arrests of Giulianis associates.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">As the indictment makes clear, neither the President nor the campaign were aware of these allegations, Sekulow said in a statement.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The two men had been major political donors to Trump. They were arrested on charges of campaign finance violations.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>1 p.m.: Trump adviser questions Chinese officials about Bidens son</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Michael Pillsbury, an informal Trump adviser who regularly consults with the president, recently asked Chinese officials questions about Hunter Biden and his business dealings, the conservative scholar said Thursday.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Most everything I learned was already public or well-known, he said. Pillsbury claimed he was told that money from the Bank of China went to Hunter Bidens firm, but that it was difficult to determine exactly how much. He said the Chinese were largely reticent to speak about Biden. They really, really didnt want to talk about it, he said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Pillsbury, who works at the conservative Hudson Institute, said he recently returned from a 10-day trip, during which he also visited Hong Kong. Pillsbury first made comments about his activities to the Financial Times.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Pillsbury said he spoke with Trump just before he went on his trip to China last month, but he said the president didnt ask him to raise Biden to Chinese officials. I havent reported back to him, no, he said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The China expert said hed never spoken with Trump about Hunter Biden but was aware of the president calling for the Chinese to investigate from the South Lawn of the White House last week.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">What a wonderful, hypothetical question, he said, when asked if he plans to report back to Trump. election.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Pillsbury regularly speaks with Trump, who calls him Mr. Pillsbury and tells others he is the worlds leading expert on China.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Josh Dawsey</i></p></div><div><div><div><hr Giuliani associates</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">House investigators issued subpoenas Thursday to the two Giuliani associates who They are not exempted from this requirement merely because they happen to work with Mr. Giuliani, and they may not defy congressional subpoenas merely because President Trump has chosen the path of denial, defiance, and obstruction.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The letter is signed by Schiff, Cummings and Engel.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>11:30 a.m.: Democrats react to arrests of Giuliani associates</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Democrats in Congress started to weigh in on the news that two men who helped Giuliani investigate Biden were arrested on charges of campaign finance violations.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Sen. Thats it.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Zelensky said he is confident of continuing American support for Ukraine, but if that changes, he expects to find out on Twitter.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Will Englund</i></p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>10:40 a.m.: Biden campaign presses case for impeachment with new video</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">A day after Biden delivered <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/joe-biden-says-president-trump-should-be-impeached-to-preserve-our-democracy/2019/10/09/d798b72e-eabf-11e9-85c0-85a098e47b37_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_236">a fiery speech in New Hampshire</a> calling for Trumps impeachment, his campaign continued to press the issue with the release of a video contending that Trump has violated the oath of his office.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The <a href="https://twitter.com/JoeBiden/status/1182304779692691456">minute-long video</a> opens with historical footage of the swearing in of past presidents  including Franklin D. Roosevelt, John F. Kennedy, Ronald Reagan and Barack Obama  before cutting to Trumps inauguration.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">It then cuts to footage of Trump calling on China to investigate the Bidens from the White House lawn before showing a clip of Bidens speech Wednesday in Rochester, N.H.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump has violated his oath of office, betrayed this nation and committed impeachable acts, Biden says in the speech.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>10:15 a.m.: Two business associates of Giuliani arrested on campaign finance charges</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Two business associates of President Trumps personal lawyer Rudolph W. Giuliani have been charged with a scheme to route foreign money into U.S. elections, according to a newly unsealed indictment.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The two men, who helped Giuliani investigate Joe Biden, were arrested Wednesday night in Virginia, according to a person familiar with the charges. The person spoke on the condition of anonymity to discuss an ongoing investigation.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Lev Parnas and Igor Fruman have been under investigation by the U.S. Attorneys office in Manhattan and are expected to appear in federal court in Virginia later on Thursday.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">According to the indictment, Parnas, Fruman and other defendants conspired to circumvent the federal laws against foreign influence by engaging in a scheme to funnel foreign money to candidates for federal and state office so that the defendants could buy potential influence with the candidates, campaigns, and the candidates governments.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The indictment also charges that Fruman and Parnas schemed to donate money to an unidentified U.S. congressman, at the same time they were asking that congressman to get the U.S. ambassador to Ukraine removed from her job.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Read more <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/two-business-associates-of-trumps-personal-lawyer-giuliani-have-been-arrested-and-are-in-custody/2019/10/10/9f9c101a-eb63-11e9-9306-47cb0324fd44_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_247">here</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Devlin Barrett</i></p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>9:10 a.m.: Trump lashes out at Fox News in response to impeachment poll finding</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump lashed out Thursday morning at Fox News in the wake of <a href="https://www.foxnews.com/politics/fox-news-poll-record-support-for-trump-impeachment">a new poll</a> that showed 51 percent of voters want to see Trump impeached and removed from office.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">From the day I announced I was running for President, I have NEVER had a good @FoxNews Poll, Trump tweeted. Whoever their Pollster is, they suck.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">He went on to contend that Fox News is much different than it used to be in the good old days, citing a number of commentators on the network who have been critical of him.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">It is so different than it used to be. Oh well, Im President! Trump said.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>9:05 a.m.: Trump seizes on comments by leader of Ukraine</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump seized on comments by Ukrainian President Volodymyr Zelensky in a Fox News report to claim that talk of impeachment should immediately end.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">As part of a day-long event with media inside a Kiev food market, Zelensky told reporters there was no blackmail when Trump pressed him to investigate the Bidens at a time when U.S. military aid was suspended.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">In his tweet, Trump quoted the lead of the Fox News story: Ukrainian President Volodymyr Zelensky told reporters Thursday his controversial July call with President Trump involved no bribe, blackmail or quid pro quo, as impeachment-minded Democrats claim.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">This should immediately end the talk of impeachment! Trump added in his own words.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>9 a.m.: House Republican leaders launch fresh attacks on Democrats over impeachment</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Top House Republicans launch fresh attacks on Democrats over impeachment on Thursday, seeking to portray the chambers leaders as so focused on ousting Trump that they are unable to get anything else done.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Democrats are so obsessed over impeaching President Trump, theyve turned their back on the border crisis, House Minority Leader Kevin McCarthy (R-Calif.) <a href="https://twitter.com/GOPLeader/status/1182278444031315969">tweeted</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">His tweet came minutes after House Minority Whip Steve Scalise (R-La.) shared a two-year-old video on Twitter of Rep. Al Green (D-Tex.) calling for Trumps removal from office.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Democrats were already trying to impeach @realDonaldTrump without a reason back in MAY 2017, Scalise <a href="https://twitter.com/SteveScalise/status/1182278037464915968">wrote</a> on Twitter. This has always been about politics and power for them  not the facts.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>8:30 a.m.: Omar re-ups impeachment call ahead of Trump rally in her district</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Omar went on Twitter on Thursday morning to preempt an expected attack on her at Trumps Minneapolis rally and to remind voters that she has called for impeaching the president.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Omar, a naturalized U.S. citizen who was born in Somalia, has been in Trumps crosshairs for months and was the subject of a send her back chant at a Trump rally in North Carolina in July.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Trump will see his rally in my district today as an opportunity to attack me, Omar <a href="https://twitter.com/IlhanMN/status/1182271599925440512">tweeted</a> Thursday morning, hours before Trump was scheduled to depart the White House. But no smear will ever stop me from working toward what Im in Congress to do.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">She listed several of her priorities, ending with Impeach Trump.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>7 a.m.: Trump hits campaign trail for first time since inquiry opened</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Ahead of his planned campaign rally in Minneapolis, Trump posted <a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/status/1182085917198241793">a video on Twitter</a> on Wednesday night that features a montage of photos from past events with large crowds of enthusiastic supporters.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The two-minute video is set to the renowned Queen song, We Will Rock You.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Thursday nights rally will be the first since House Speaker Nancy Pelosi (D-Calif.) announced the impeachment inquiry against Trump on Sept. 24.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">It marks a rare campaign appearance in a state that Trump did not carry in 2016. His campaign, however, is pouring significant resources into Minnesota in hopes of putting it into play next year.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>6 a.m.: George Conway and other prominent conservatives call for expeditious impeachment probe</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">More than a dozen prominent conservative lawyers, including George T. Conway III, offered their legal reasoning for an expeditious impeachment probe into Trump, creating a document they hope will be read by Republicans who continue to stand by the president.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">The 16 attorneys, many of whom worked in Republican administrations, wrote in a joint statement released Thursday morning that Trumps now infamous call with Zelensky, the text messages between diplomats and Trumps public call for China to investigate a political opponent are undisputed events that amount to Trump violating his oath of office.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">We have not just a political candidate open to receiving foreign assistance to better his chances at winning an election, but a current president openly and privately calling on foreign governments to actively interfere in the most sacred of U.S. democratic processes, our elections, they wrote.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Read more <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/george-conway-and-other-prominent-conservatives-call-for-expeditious-impeachment-probe/2019/10/09/4971b404-eade-11e9-9c6d-436a0df4f31d_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_284">here</a>.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>5:45 a.m.: Biden campaign slams New York Times for op-ed by conservative author behind Ukraine claims</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">As Trump has lobbed unsubstantiated and false claims of international corruption at Biden and his son, hes often turned to one source for ammunition: conservative author Peter Schweizer.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">So when the New York Times ran an op-ed on Wednesday written by Schweizer about the Bidens, the Democratic presidential candidates campaign cried foul.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">In a letter sent to New York Times executive editor Dean Baquet, Bidens campaign called Schweizer a discredited right-wing polemicist and suggested the op-ed was part of a larger pattern of journalistic malpractice.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Are you truly blind to what you got wrong in 2016, or are you deliberately continuing policies that distort reality for the sake of controversy and the clicks that accompany it? Kate Bedingfield, Bidens deputy campaign manager, wrote in the Wednesday letter.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Read more <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/nation/2019/10/10/joe-biden-peter-schweizer-new-york-times-op-ed/?tid=lk_inline_manual_291">here</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Tim Elfrink</i></p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>6:30 a.m.: 51 percent of voters want Trump removed from office, Fox News poll finds</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">A Fox News poll is the latest to show growing support for ousting Trump.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Fifty-one percent of voters want Trump impeached and removed from office, according to <a href="https://www.foxnews.com/politics/fox-news-poll-record-support-for-trump-impeachment">the poll</a> released Wednesday night.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">That number has risen from 42 percent in a July poll by the network.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Fox noted that support for impeachment has risen since July among several of Trumps key constituencies, including white evangelical Christians (up five percentage points), white men without a college degree (up eight points) and rural whites (up 10 points).</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Support for impeaching Trump and removing him from office has ranged from 43 percent to 48 percent in <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/poll-majority-of-americans-say-they-endorse-opening-of-house-impeachment-inquiry-of-trump/2019/10/07/be9e0af6-e936-11e9-85c0-85a098e47b37_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_299">other independent national polls</a> released this week.</p></div><div><div><div><hr style="margin-top:-10px;margin-bottom:-10px;"/></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><b>5 a.m.: Ousted Ukraine envoy expected to testify in impeachment probe despite White House vow not to cooperate, congressional aides say</b></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Congressional investigators expect that Marie Yovanovitch, the former ambassador to Ukraine, will appear as planned for a Friday deposition in the Houses ongoing impeachment inquiry, despite the White Houses emphatic pledge not to cooperate with Democrats efforts to investigate Trump, according to congressional officials involved with the process.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Yovanovitch and her lawyer are on board, according to a senior congressional aide, who like others spoke on the condition of anonymity to discuss sensitive negotiations. State Department officials would not address questions about the matter, and efforts to contact Yovanovitch on Wednesday were unsuccessful.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">White House lawyer Pat Cipollone issued a letter to Democrats on Tuesday outlining the Trump administrations objections to the impeachment inquiry, calling it unconstitutional and vowing to reject congressional requests to cooperate.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">House Democrats have deposed only Trumps former special envoy to Ukraine, Kurt Volker, who resigned his post late last month and then provided the committees with copies of text messages he exchanged with other diplomats, Trump personal lawyer Rudolph W. Giuliani and a top aide to Zelensky.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined">Read more <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/ousted-ukraine-envoy-expected-to-testify-in-impeachment-probe-despite-white-house-vow-not-to-cooperate-congressional-aides-say/2019/10/09/c46aebe8-eabc-11e9-85c0-85a098e47b37_story.html?tid=lk_inline_manual_306">here</a>.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy color-gray-darkest ma-0 pad-bottom-md undefined"><i> Karoun Demirjian and Carol Morello</i></p></div></section></div></div><div class="mb-lg pad-bottom-xs pad-top-xs"
